# Non-resonant hh -> bbtautau - Chris Deutsch - 31-01-2019
# Cross sections and branching ratios from LHCHXSWG (mH = 125 GeV)
# XS = 2 * 2 * Br(H->bb) * Br(H->tautau) * XS(HH)
# XS = 2 * 2 * 5.824e-1  * 6.272e-2      * 31.05 fb = 4.5367934976 fb
# Factor 4 because:
# - Two possible orientations for the Higgs decay (i.e. HH -> bbtt & HH -> ttbb)
# - Generate all of bbbb, bbtt, ttbb, tttt with equal probabilty but filtering out bbtt & ttbb
# DSID   XS(pb)         K-factor      Filter Eff.
